        <h4 class="category-title box-article-content--category" data-href="/our-transformation">
         Our Transformation
        </h4>
        <h2 class="title4 box-article-content--title button-present">
         Delivering a smoke-free future
        </h2>
        <p class="box-article-content--description">
         We're one of the world's leading tobacco companies, and we're committed to finding alternatives to cigarettes as quickly as possible.
        </p>
        <small class="box-article-content--reading small-style">
         5 min read

      <div class="small-text-on-image--content">
       <h2 class="title8 box-article-content--title">
        U.S. FDA authorizes IQOS as a modified risk tobacco product
       </h2>
       <p class="box-article-content--description">
        PMI's smoke-free innovation becomes the first and only electronic nicotine product to receive such authorization.
       </p>
       <div class="box-article-content--link category-title arrow-link">
        Read Article
       </div>

         <h2 class="title4 box-article-content--title">
          Scientific research
         </h2>
         <p class="box-article-content--description">
          Applying rigorous standards. Inviting independent verification.
